The Portmantout
A portmanteau of every word in English

Hi, for the prestigious conference SIGBOVIK 2015 I built some software to create a portmanteau (which is where you jam two words together, like caviar+armpits = caviarmpits) of all of the words in the English language. It's called a "portmantout", since "tout" means "all" in French. You can read this short paper about it, or watch this video (which is intended to be fun, but, I guess it depends on what kind of person you are):

You could download the source code or word list for your own explorations.

Since writing the paper I've improved my portmantout a bit; this one is "only" 611,820 letters:
